### To scrape
- [Scrapy](https://scrapy.org/)  
- [Quotes to Scrape](http://quotes.toscrape.com/)  
- [Books to Scrape](http://books.toscrape.com/)  
- [Beautiful Soup 4 no PyPI](https://pypi.org/project/beautifulsoup4/)  
- [Documentação Beautiful Soup 4](https://beautiful-soup-4.readthedocs.io/en/latest/)  
- [lxml no PyPI](https://pypi.org/project/lxml/)  
- [Documentação lxml](https://lxml.de/)

## Comandos

```python
python3 -m venv .venv
source .venv/bin/activate
pip3 install scrapy
python3 quotes.py # (ou scrapy startproject quotes_scrapy e em seguida scrapy crawl quotes -o quotes.json)
# Opcional:
pip3 install beautifulsoup4 lxml
```

-----

## Spiders para crawlers

**Spider1:**

```python
def print_spider1():
    print("************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""             ;               ,              """, flush=True)
    print("""           ,;                 '.            """, flush=True)
    print("""          ;:                   :;           """, flush=True)
    print("""         ::                     ::          """, flush=True)
    print("""         ::                     ::          """, flush=True)
    print("""         ':                     :           """, flush=True)
    print("""          :.                    :           """, flush=True)
    print("""       ;' ::                   ::  '        """, flush=True)
    print("""      .'  ';                   ;'  '.       """, flush=True)
    print("""     ::    :;                 ;:    ::      """, flush=True)
    print("""     ;      :;.             ,;:     ::      """, flush=True)
    print("""     :;      :;:           ,;"      ::      """, flush=True)
    print("""     ::.      ':;  ..,.;  ;:'     ,.;:      """, flush=True)
    print("""      "'"...   '::,::::: ;:   .;.;""'       """, flush=True)
    print("""          '""'....;:::::;, ;.;'""           """, flush=True)
    print("""      .:::.....'"':::::::'",...;::::;.      """, flush=True)
    print("""     ;:' '""'"";.,;:::::;.'""""""  ':;      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ::'         ;::;:::;::..         :;     """, flush=True)
    print("""   ::         ,;:::::::::::;:..       ::    """, flush=True)
    print("""   ;'     ,;;:;::::::::::::::;";..    ':.   """, flush=True)
    print("""  ::     ;:"  ::::::''''::::::  ":     ::   """, flush=True)
    print("""   :.    ::   :::::: :: ::::::   :     ;    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ;    ::   :::::: :: ::::::   :    ;     """, flush=True)
    print("""     '   ::   ::::::....:::::'  ,:   '      """, flush=True)
    print("""      '  ::    :::::::::::::"   ::          """, flush=True)
    print("""         ::     ':::::::::"'    ::          """, flush=True)
    print("""         ':       """""""'      ::          """, flush=True)
    print("""          ::                   ;:           """, flush=True)
    print("""          ':;                 ;:"           """, flush=True)
    print("""            ';              ,;'             """, flush=True)
    print("""              "'           '"               """, flush=True)
    print("""                '                           """, flush=True)
    print("************************************************", flush=True)
```

**Spider2:**

```python
def print_spider2():
    print("**********************************************", flush=True)
    print("""                                          """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣾⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢨⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠠⡃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢰⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⣇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣸⡆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡇    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢸⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⠇    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠘⣧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠹⣆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣰⠏⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠹⣧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠸⣧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⡏⠀⠀⠀⠀⣰⠏⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠹⣧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⣷⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣾⠍⠀⠀⠀⠀⣴⠏⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⡧⣀⠀⠀⠀⠘⣿⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⣾⠏⠀⠀⠀⣀⣼⠏⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠙⠻⣶⣤⡀⠘⢿⡄⣀⣀⢠⣿⠃⠀⣠⣴⡾⠛⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⠻⢷⣜⣿⣿⣿⣿⣣⣶⠿⠋⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣠⣤⣽⣿⣿⣿⣿⣯⣅⣀⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣤⣴⠾⠿⠛⢋⣥⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣍⠛⠻⠿⢶⣤⣄⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⢰⡟⠉⠀⠀⠀⣠⡾⣻⢟⣥⣶⣿⣿⣿⡿⣷⣄⠀⠀⠈⠀⢿⡄⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⢠⡟⠀⠀⠀⣠⡾⠋⢰⣯⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡈⠻⣷⣄⠀⠀⠈⢷⡀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⢀⡾⠁⠀⠀⣼⠋⠀⠀⢸⢸⣿⡿⠿⣿⠿⣿⣿⡇⠀⠈⢫⣧⠀⠀⠘⣷⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⣼⠃⠀⠀⢠⣿⠀⠀⠀⠸⣿⣿⣿⡆⠀⣼⡟⣹⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⠀⠀⠀⠸⣧⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⡟⠀⠀⠀⢸⡏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⢿⣯⣶⣶⣮⡿⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⢹⡇⠀⠀⠀⣿⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⡇⠀⠀⠀⣼⠇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠛⠋⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣇⠀⠀⠀⢸⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⡇⠀⠀⠀⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⣿⠀⠀⠀⢸⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⡇⠀⠀⠀⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⠀⠀⠀⢸⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⡇⠀⠀⠀⢸⡆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⡏⠀⠀⠀⢸⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣸⠁⠀⠀⠀⠈⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠸⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡸⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""                                          """, flush=True)
    print("**********************************************", flush=True)
```

**Spider3:**

```python
def print_spider3():
    print("*********************************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""                                                                 """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣠⣴⡞⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⣞⣥⠞⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⡞⢉⡟⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⣤⣒⣉⠐⡶⠲⢤⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡞⢀⡾⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠉⠉⠛⢶⣄⣈⣳⣄⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⠧⢾⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠉⢷⡀⠑⡄⠀⠀⠀⡏⢀⡾⠀⠀⠀⣀⣤⠤⠤⠤⢄⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⣴⣎⣉⠐⢶⠦⠤⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⣦⠼⣆⠀⢰⠓⢺⡇⣠⡴⠋⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⡆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠈⠋⠁⠀⠉⠙⠛⠶⣤⣀⢙⡟⢦⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡀⠸⡄⡆⠀⣿⣴⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠻⣥⣄⡼⠛⢢⡀⠀⠀⢳⣀⣇⣇⢀⡟⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⠦⣄⡙⢢⣀⢸⢋⣉⣿⣽⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⡞⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⢻⣁⣨⠟⠉⠁⠀⠀⢣⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⣴⣋⠤⠴⡶⠤⠔⠒⠲⣤⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡤⠤⢤⡔⠊⠉⠉⠉⣺⠉⡽⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⡶⢶⡶⠒⠋⣿⣉⣀⣀⡴⠷⠶⠶⠤⠖⠻⢦⣉⣐⣄⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⠴⠒⠋⠉⣧⣤⠴⠓⠒⠒⠒⠛⢙⡿⠀⣤⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⠽⣶⣗⣚⣉⠉⠉⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠻⢧    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⡤⠚⢉⣹⠶⠒⠋⠉⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡠⢂⡽⣧⠸⠍⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣰⡞⣶⣿⣤⣄⣹⡉⠉⠉⠑⣶⢄⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢀⣾⡤⠚⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⣷⠋⠀⠹⣇⣀⢶⣾⣧⣴⠋⣹⣿⣏⠙⢄⠀⠈⠉⠉⠛⠚⠳⢦⣈⣑⣦⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠈⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠸⠃⠀⠀⠀⠈⣹⢟⡿⠃⠙⣏⠉⢳⡹⣦⣈⣧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⢷⡄⢣⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⣴⣾⠿⠋⠀⠀⠀⠹⣆⣠⡇⢻⡇⢻⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⣿⠄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⠁⢣⢸⣇⣠⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠛⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⣀⣈⡆⣿⠀⣇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⠁⡟⠀⢸⣧⡼⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    ⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢿⠀⢣⠀⢺⠀⡿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡧⡼⠀⣾⡖⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢿⠀⣿⠀⠛⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣠⠏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣾⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""                                                                 """, flush=True)
    print("*********************************************************************", flush=True)
```

```python
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠁⠀⠀⢀⣠⣾⡿⠟⢋⣹⣿⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⣿⣯⡙⠻⠿⣷⣄⡀⠀⠀⠈⠉⠁⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣴⠾⠋⠁⣠⣴⡾⠋⠁⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⠈⠙⢿⣦⣄⠈⠙⠷⣦⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
```

**Spider5:**

```python
def print_spider5():
    print("*********************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⣹⣿⡿⢹⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡏⢿⣿⣏⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)   
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡟⢰⣿⡿⠁⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡈⢿⣿⡆⠻⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠏⢠⣿⣿⠃⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣇⠘⣿⣿⡄⠹⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⡟⠀⣾⣿⠇⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⠸⣿⣷⠀⢹⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⠁⢸⣿⡿⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⢿⣿⡇⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⣿⣿⠇⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⠸⣿⣿⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⠀⠀⣿⣿⠀⠀⠘⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⢿⣿⠿⣿⣿⠿⣿⡿⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⠃⠀⠀⣿⣿⠀⠀⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⡇⠀⢰⣿⣿⣿⣦⡶⠶⠖⠋⠉⠛⠦⠀⠉⠐⠙⠋⠃⠈⠀⠴⠛⠉⠙⠲⠶⢶⣴⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⢸⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⡀⠀⠈⠛⠉⠉⣀⣀⣤⣴⠶⢶⣦⡤⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢤⣤⡶⠶⣦⣤⣀⣀⠉⠉⠛⠁⠀⢀⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣦⣄⣴⣶⣿⣿⣿⠟⠁⢀⣠⣤⠄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠠⣤⣄⡀⠈⠻⣿⣿⣿⣶⣦⣠⣴⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠛⠁⣀⣴⡿⠟⠁⣠⡔⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢲⣄⠈⠻⢿⣦⣀⠈⠛⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠟⠋⢀⣤⣾⣿⡇⠀⠀⣴⣿⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢨⣿⣦⠀⠀⢸⣿⣷⣤⡀⠙⠻⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⡿⣿⠿⠋⠁⣠⣴⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⠀⣿⣿⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣿⣿⠀⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣦⣄⠈⠙⠿⣿⠿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⡇⠀⠀⣴⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⠀⣿⣿⣷⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣾⣿⣿⠀⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣦⠀⠀⢠    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⡇⠀⢰⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⠀⣿⣿⣿⡆⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⣿⣿⣿⠀⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡆⠀⢸    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⡇⠀⠈⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⡀⠀⠀⢀⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠁⠀⢸    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⠀⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣀⣀⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⠀⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⡄⠀⢻⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣇⠀⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⠀⣸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠀⢠⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣧⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⣼⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣇⠈⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡆⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⢠⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠁⣰⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⡄⢹⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣇⠀⢻⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠀⣸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡏⢠⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⡈⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⢀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⢁⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⡘⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣇⠈⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠁⣸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⢇⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡆⢹⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡏⢠⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡌⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⢡⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣜⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣣⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿    """, flush=True)
    print("*********************************************************", flush=True)
```

**Spider6:**

```python

    print("********************************************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""                                                                            """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡤⠂⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣀⣤⠔⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠢⣤⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠐⣤⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)

    print("""                                                                            """, flush=True)
    print("********************************************************************************", flush=True)
```

**Spider7:**

```python
def print_spider7():
    print("*************************************************************************", flush=True)

    print(""" ⠀⢸⢸⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⣿⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⣿⣿⣵⣶⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣾⡿⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠸⣿⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡇⡀⠀""", flush=True)
```

**Spider9:**

```python
def print_spider9():
    print("*****************************************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""                                                                         """, flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀ """, flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⣾⠿⠿⣷⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)

    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣰⣿⠏⠀⠈⣻⣿⠏⠀⠀⠀⣸⣿⣷⣶⣶⡿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣿⠉⠛⠛⣿⠇⠀⢸⣿⠀⠀⣈⣛⠀⠀⠀⠀⠸⣿⣆⣤⣶⣿⣿⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)

    print("*****************************************************************************", flush=True)
```

**Spider10:**

```python
def print_spider10():
    print("********************************************************************************************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""                                                                                                                            """, flush=True)
    print("""                                                                                                                            """, flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⣾⠓⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⣿⣡⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣤⡿⢣⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)

    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢻⡇⠆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢂⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠛⣿⣿⣷⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⣿⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⣾⡇⣀⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣷⢡⠂⡁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠐⠀⠂⢀⠀⠐⠀⢂⠀⠀⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠸⣿⣷⡻⠖⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⣿⠏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⣿⢇⠿⠃""", flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣞⢿⣦⣠⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⢀⡀⠀⠄⠀⠀⠄⠂⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠚⣿⣿⡤⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣾⡏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣿⠂⠀⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠻⣷⡦⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠐⠀⠠⢄⠀⠌⢀⠂⠃⠌⠠⠀⠤⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⣿⣿⡈⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣸⡟⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣸⠇⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⠂⡃⠤⠄⠂⢆⡐⠀⠈⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠀⠀⠀⠠⠀⠀⠈⢿⣷⣂⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣿⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠏⠀⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡀⠢⠡⠐⢊⠁⠖⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠐⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⢷⡂⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠐⠏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⠀⠀⠀⠄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠄⠠⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠀⢁⠁⠈⠂⠉⠈⠂⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠳⠶⠤⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠠⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠠⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠐⠂⠀⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠂⠀⠐⠀⠠⢀⠂⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""                                                                                                                            """, flush=True)
    print("********************************************************************************************************************************", flush=True)
```

**Pirate:**

```python
def print_pirate():
    print("********************************************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣰⣿⣷⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣴⣿⣿⣿⠀⠀⢀⣠⣤⣶⣶⣶⣶⣶⣶⣶⣦⣤⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣀⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⡔⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⢟⣫⣯⣷⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⡙⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⢋⣵⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣧⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣀⣤⣶⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣦⣙⠿⠿⠿⢟⣫⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⢹⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣤⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⢸⣿⣿⣿⡏⠉⠙⢿⣿⣿⣦⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣴⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⣿⡿⡍⠳⣄⡀⢀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⢀⣼⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⢿⣿⢿⡄⠸⡿⢄⠛⣘⢠⣼⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣧⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⡞⣼⡻⡄⠳⡤⠽⠾⠿⠿⠿⢛⣻⣿⣿⣿⣷⡀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⢻⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣾⣿⣿⣄⠙⢶⣶⣶⣶⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣧⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠻⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠟⠛⠉⢉⣁⣀⣀⣀⣀⣀⣉⡉⠙⠛⠻⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣯⣻⣍⡲⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡄⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⢀⡀⣶⣤⣌⢻⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠿⠋⣁⣤⣶⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣶⣤⣈⠛⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠟⠛⠛⠁⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣰⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣝⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣟⣡⣶⠿⢛⣛⣉⣭⣭⣤⣤⡴⠶⠶⠶⠶⢲⣴⣤⠭⠭⡭⣟⠻⠦⣝⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠟⢉⣀⣠⣶⣿⣆⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠹⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣙⠻⣿⣮⣛⠿⣿⣿⣿⣫⣵⡶⠟⣛⣋⣭⣭⣶⣶⣶⣶⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣶⣾⣮⣽⣿⣿⣿⠿⠟⠛⠉⢀⣴⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣶⡀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠈⠙⠋⠁⠀⠈⠉⠛⠳⣭⣛⢷⣦⣸⣿⣯⣶⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡏⣿⠀⠀⠀⣀⣴⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⡟⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣠⣾⣿⣿⠿⠿⢿⣹⣿⣧⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⢸⡏⣀⣴⣾⣿⣿⠿⠛⠉⠀⠀⠀⠈⠛⠛⠉⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣴⠿⠛⠋⠁⠀⠀⠀⢀⣯⢿⣿⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⣿⠣⣟⡻⠟⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣀⣴⣾⣿⠈⡿⣿⠃⠀⠀⠀⠈⠉⠛⠻⠿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠿⠛⠉⠉⠀⠈⠉⠛⣿⣽⡟⠋⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣠⣤⣶⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣀⣼⣿⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣹⡟⣻⣿⡃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢹⣷⣤⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⢀⣴⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⢹⣿⣿⣿⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣰⣿⢣⡇⣿⣷⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⣿⣿⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠟⠋⠙⠛⠻⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠏⠀⠈⢿⣿⣿⣿⣦⣄⣀⣀⣀⣠⣴⣿⣏⡞⢻⣸⣿⣷⣄⠀⠀⣀⣤⠴⣾⣿⣿⣿⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⣿⣿⠃⠀⠀⠀⠈⢿⣿⣵⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⠀⠀⠹⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣶⠾⠋⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⣏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣼⣿⡛⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠟⣡⣾⣆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⠀⠀⢠⣶⣿⣿⣯⣿⡇⠀⢹⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣤⣤⣦⣶⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⣿⣿⢸⣿⣶⣤⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣄⣠⣴⣾⣿⣟⣿⠟⠁⣿⡇⠀⣿⡿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡏⡇⢀⣿⣿⠙⢮⣛⠿⣷⣦⣄⣀⣀⣀⣠⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⣴⣶⣶⣾⣿⣿⡿⣛⣽⠞⠋⠀⠀⠀⣿⣷⠀⣍⠇⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠿⠉⡄⣸⣿⡿⠀⠀⠈⠙⠮⣟⠿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣹⣿⣿⣿⢵⡿⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢿⣿⣦⣿⡷⣄⠙⠿⣿⢹⣿⣿⢼⡿⠋⣡⣶⣳⣿⣿⣿⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠿⠬⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠸⣿⣿⣿⣿⠟⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠻⣿⣿⣷⣻⢿⣶⣬⣈⣉⣉⣤⣴⣿⣻⣾⣿⣿⠟⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢿⣿⣿⡿⠇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⠋⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠻⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⣿⣇⣿⢹⣿⣿⣿⣿⡟⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀   ⡀⡁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀        """, flush=True)
```

**Hacker:**

```python
def print_hacker():
    print("***********************************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⡠⢤⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡴⠟⠃⠀⠀⠙⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⣆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⠾⢛⠒⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⣶⣄⡈⠓⢄⠠⡀⠀⠀⠀⣄⣷⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀       """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣿⣷⠀⠈⠱⡄⠑⣌⠆⠀⠀⡜⢻⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣿⡿⠳⡆⠐⢿⣆⠈⢿⠀⠀⡇⠘⡆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢿⣿⣷⡇⠀⠀⠈⢆⠈⠆⢸⠀⠀⢣⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀       """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⣿⣿⣿⣧⠀⠀⠈⢂⠀⡇⠀⠀⢨⠓⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣸⣿⣿⣿⣦⣤⠖⡏⡸⠀⣀⡴⠋⠀⠈⠢⡀⠀⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⣾⠁⣹⣿⣿⣿⣷⣾⠽⠖⠊⢹⣀⠄⠀⠀⠀⠈⢣⡀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡟⣇⣰⢫⢻⢉⠉⠀⣿⡆⠀⠀⡸⡏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢇      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢨⡇⡇⠈⢸⢸⢸⠀⠀⡇⡇⠀⠀⠁⠻⡄⡠⠂⠀⠀⠀⠘      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢤⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⠛⠓⡇⠀⠸⡆⢸⠀⢠⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⣰⣿⣵⡆⠀⠀⠀⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠈⢻⣷⣦⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⡿⣦⣀⡇⠀⢧⡇⠀⠀⢺⡟⠀⠀⠀⢰⠉⣰⠟⠊⣠⠂⠀⡸      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⢻⣿⣿⣷⣦⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⢧⡙⠺⠿⡇⠀⠘⠇⠀⠀⢸⣧⠀⠀⢠⠃⣾⣌⠉⠩⠭⠍⣉⡇      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠻⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣦⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⣞⣋⠀⠈⠀⡳⣧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡏⠀⠀⡞⢰⠉⠉⠉⠉⠉⠓⢻⠃      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⡄⠀⠀⢀⣀⠠⠤⣤⣤⠤⠞⠓⢠⠈⡆⠀⢣⣸⣾⠆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣀⡼⠁⡿⠈⣉⣉⣒⡒⠢⡼⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣎⣽⣶⣤⡶⢋⣤⠃⣠⡦⢀⡼⢦⣾⡤⠚⣟⣁⣀⣀⣀⣀⠀⣀⣈⣀⣠⣾⣅⠀⠑⠂⠤⠌⣩⡇⠀      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡁⣺⢁⣞⣉⡴⠟⡀⠀⠀⠀⠁⠸⡅⠀⠈⢷⠈⠏⠙⠀⢹⡛⠀⢉⠀⠀⠀⣀⣀⣼⡇⠀      """, flush=True)

    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠻⣿⣿⡄⠈⠻⣿⣿⢿⣛⣩⠤⠒⠉⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠒⢤⡀⠉⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡿⠀⠀⠀      """, flush=True)
```

**Snake1:**

```python
def print_snake1():
    print("*************************************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣀⣤⣴⢶⣾⣞⠒⠶⢤⣀⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)        
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⡟⢩⣇⠀⢛⣿⡟⠀⠀⠀⠙⢿⡲⢤⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⣿⡒⡳⠒⠚⠙⠒⠂⠀⠀⠰⡄⢹⡄⢟⢷⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠉⢹⡿⠶⣶⣤⡤⠤⠤⠖⢿⠁⣹⣺⡾⠈⢷⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⡇⠀⠀⠘⣗⡒⠒⠒⢺⡏⣹⣽⡇⢰⠀⢳⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⠇⠀⠀⡄⢿⣉⠑⠒⢚⣏⣹⠉⡟⡞⢀⡎⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⠀⠀⠀⢧⣾⣮⣉⠒⢺⠋⡟⢺⣷⠛⣟⡼⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⡏⠀⠀⣇⣼⣾⠃⠈⠁⡏⢸⠷⣇⣼⠚⠋⠀⡟⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣿⠀⣠⢀⣟⣡⡏⠀⠀⣸⠁⣿⣟⣩⡄⢀⠀⣸⠇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣿⣠⠿⣼⢛⡟⠀⠀⢠⠃⢸⣟⡽⣥⠷⡜⣶⡟⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡇⢹⣶⢯⢯⣉⠒⠶⡞⣠⣿⢯⡴⢧⢼⣿⠏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⣷⣾⣸⠻⢤⣈⠉⣻⠉⢠⣇⣾⣷⣿⠟⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⣿⠃⠀⠀⠀⣰⠃⢀⡿⣻⣿⠟⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣼⠋⠀⠀⠀⢠⠇⢀⣾⠟⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣾⠏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⡏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣿⠏⢠⡿⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣠⠴⠶⠶⠶⠤⣄⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣾⡏⠀⠀⠻⣝⠷⣄⣀⣀⣀⣤⠶⠛⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⢻⡙⢶⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣀⣀⣀⣀⣀⠀⢸⡇⡀⠘⢦⣰⢃⣸⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⢷⣄⣀⣩⣥⡤⠤⠦⠦⠤⢤⣤⣤⣤⣴⡶⠏⠀⠀⠙⡆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⣠⡴⠞⠛⠉⢀⡠⠆⠀⠉⠙⢻⡇⠙⠢⣄⣿⣁⣼⣿⣤⠤⠤⠶⠛⠛⠉⠁⠀⣀⣀⣠⡤⠤⠤⠴⢶⠤⠴⠦⠤⣤⣀⣀⣴⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⢀⡞⠁⠀⠀⠀⢠⡎⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡇⠲⣄⡀⠙⣇⣼⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣤⠶⠚⠛⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠙⠓⢦⡀⠀⠀⠙⠛⠦⣤⡀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢠⡟⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣄⣤⣤⢤⣤⣀⣸⡇⠀⠀⠉⣋⣯⣸⣿⣤⡤⠞⠋⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢹⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⢧⡀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢸⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⢿⣉⠀⠀⠀⠉⠛⣿⠤⢤⣀⠈⠙⣤⡿⣧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣀⣀⣤⣤⣤⣀⣸⣿⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⣷⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠸⣧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⠛⠒⠒⠚⠛⢻⡆⠠⣄⣉⣉⣹⡼⢻⣧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣠⣤⠶⠟⠛⠋⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣹⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣹⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠘⢷⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢻⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⣍⠈⠳⣦⣴⡾⠿⠛⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⡼⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⡿⡀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠙⠷⣤⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠻⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠳⡄⠀⠉⠛⠲⠤⠤⣤⣀⣀⣤⠤⠤⠤⠔⠚⠋⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⣿⠃⠀    """, flush=True)

    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠳⢦⣀⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣤⣶⠟⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠙⠒⠲⠤⠤⢤⣄⣀⣀⣀⣀⣀⣀⣠⣤⣤⣤⡤⠶⠶⠛⠛⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)

    print("*************************************************************************", flush=True)
```

**Snake2:**

```python
def print_snake2():
    print("*****************************************************************", flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⢀⣀⣀⣀⣀⣠⣤⣤⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    ⠀""", flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⣿⣿⣿⣏⠉⠈⣿⣿⣿⢦⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣀⣀⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⢿⠋⠻⣿⣷⣄⡙⠛⠋⠀⠈⠹⣷⠚⠛⣟⠽⣯⠝⠋⠙⣶⣄⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠉⠙⢿⠲⠤⣼⡿⡆⠀⢢⠀⠉⠲⠏⠀⠀⠀⣇⢻⠙⣆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡇⢀⡼⠁⠀⠀⢸⠟⠉⠉⠛⢦⠀⠀⢿⡼⠿⡚⣇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⢀⣠⣶⡶⠿⢿⡿⣿⠟⢁⣀⣠⠔⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⢻⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⢀⣾⡞⠁⢀⣴⡯⠞⣡⡴⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣰⠃⠀⠀⠀⣠⠄⣸⠆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠈⠙⠀⠀⢿⣤⠤⠞⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡼⠃⢰⡖⠒⢤⣧⣤⣼⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⠖⠋⠀⠀⠈⡧⠀⣏⠁⢰⠇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⠴⠋⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠓⢦⣷⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡴⠚⠁⠀⠀⢴⠒⠒⠢⡀⠀⠀⢠⠞⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⠶⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡼⢀⡶⠆⢳⣤⠔⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡴⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠸⡀⠹⣀⣸⠞⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡼⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⡶⠛⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣠⠴⠒⢿⡉⠛⢍⠛⠒⢤⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⡤⢤⣀⣠⠎⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡴⢯⡀⠀⠀⠀⢹⡆⠻⠦⠴⠃⢈⣣⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣼⣀⡖⣾⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⡾⢅⣸⠁⠀⠀⠀⠸⡦⠖⠤⣀⠜⠁⠈⢷⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⡟⠀⠀⠀⠀⡏⠹⡗⢺⢻⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⠿⠖⣉⣀⣱⠀⣀⡤⠤⢤⣄⠀⠀⠀⢀⣀⣸⠀⠀⠀⠐⠻⣗⠲⣄⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠉⠉⢹⠚⢷⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⡴⠛⠒⠊⠀⠀⣠⠎⠁⠀⠀⠀⠈⢳⡀⠀⣿⣸⡿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⣇⠘⡆    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠸⡇⢸⠙⡟⠲⡖⠋⣯⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡧⣎⣈⣿⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⣆⢻    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢷⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⡇⢼⡤⠃⡔⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⣸⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⡇⠀⠀⣯⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⠷⠼⢺    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⢳⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠐⠖⠚⠒⠞⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣰⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢷⠀⠸⠽⠷⣄⣀⣀⣠⡶⠋⠀⢠⡟    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠳⣄⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⠞⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠳⣄⠀⠀⢯⡛⡷⠚⠁⢀⡴⠋⠀    """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠙⠒⠒⠦⠤⠤⠤⠴⠖⠚⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠙⠒⠲⠿⠷⠒⠛⠉⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("*****************************************************************", flush=True)⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀
```

**Snake3:**

```python
def print_snake3():
    print("**************************************************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""                                                                                  """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⣤⠶⢖⣚⣋⣭⣿⠍⠉⠙⠲⠶⣤⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣰⠾⠋⠁⢀⡾⢋⡼⠛⠁⠀⣀⡤⠤⠤⢤⣀⠙⢷⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)

    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⣷⠀⣠⡾⡆⠀⠈⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⢿⣿⡷⣶⠶⠹⣦⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢹    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣀⣤⣿⠘⠛⠛⠟⠀⠀⢻⡷⢶⡶⠤⠤⣤⣄⣀⣀⣀⣀⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠸⣟⠋⠉⠀⠀⠹⣆⠀⠀⠀⠀⡀⠀⠀⢸    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣠⣤⡶⢾⣿⣛⡉⢉⣿⠀⢀⣤⠾⡇⠀⠘⡇⠘⢿⠓⢶⡤⠀⠉⢩⣭⣽⣿⣛⠓⠶⢦⣤⣤⣤⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⡦⠐⠒⠉⠀⠀⠀⢸    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣠⡴⠾⢛⣍⣀⣀⠈⠻⣏⡿⢸⡇⠠⠿⠶⢦⡇⠀⠀⣿⡀⠈⠷⠟⠀⠀⠀⠀⠹⣄⢀⡽⠿⠃⠀⢰⡶⠬⢭⣹⡻⠶⣼⡏⣾⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⢿⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⣀⣴⠟⢫⣴⣾⠯⢭⣍⣻⡄⠀⠘⠃⢸⡇⠀⠀⠀⢀⣤⣤⡀⠘⣧⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢿⠏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣧⣤⣤⠾⠁⢠⣿⣾⠁⠻⣤⡀⠀⠀⠸⡇⠀⠀⢀⡀⠀⢸    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⢀⣾⠟⠁⠀⠈⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠹⠇⠀⠀⠀⠈⣿⠀⠀⢰⣿⠷⣬⣷⠀⠘⢷⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠁⠀⢀⣴⠟⠈⠙⠲⠶⣮⣿⡦⠀⠀⣇⠀⠉⠁⠀⠀⣾    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢠⡿⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⡤⣤⣘⣧⠀⠀⠀⢀⣀⣸⣆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢼⣇⠀⠀⠙⢿⣛⠛⠻⠶⠶⠤⣤⣀⣀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣠⠾⢋⣡⢴⡄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢹⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠⡇    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣾⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣼⠃⣠⡤⠿⠛⢷⣴⣿⣋⣉⣤⡽⣧⣀⠀⢠⣴⣿⣿⣿⡦⠀⠀⠉⠛⢦⣤⣄⣀⣀⣠⣭⡿⠗⠚⠋⠡⣾⠋⠁⢸⣇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣼⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⠃    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣷⠞⠉⠀⠀⣤⠾⠛⠻⣿⠉⠉⠉⢉⣿⣛⣒⣒⠒⠒⠒⢲⡒⠒⢒⡒⡒⠛⠉⢉⣉⣡⣤⠶⢷⡄⠀⠀⠹⣆⠀⠀⠹⣆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢰⣧⣤⡤⢄⣼⠃⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢸⣆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡇⠀⢀⡾⠃⠀⠀⢀⡾⠉⠉⣹⠟⠀⠀⠀⣼⠋⠉⠉⣹⡇⠀⠀⢸⡏⠀⠀⠀⢸⡇⠀⠀⠀⠉⠳⢤⣀⣙⣦⡀⠀⠀⠀⢀⡿⠁⠀⢀⣼⠋⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠙⣆⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡇⢠⡟⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡇⠀⣴⡏⠀⠀⠀⠀⢿⠀⠀⢰⠟⠀⠀⠀⠀⢷⠀⠀⠀⣸⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠛⠋⠀⠀⢀⡾⠁⠀⣠⣿⠃⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠈⢷⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣷⡟⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡇⣰⡏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⡀⠀⣿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⢷⡀⠀⡏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣰⠞⠒⣶⣾⠟⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠙⠦⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠛⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠻⠿⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢷⣼⡏⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠻⣦⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣠⠾⣃⣠⡾⠟⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠛⠦⣤⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠿⠃⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠁⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣀⣴⣺⣥⠿⠟⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠛⠶⢦⣤⣀⣀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣠⣴⣾⠿⠛⠉⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠉⠙⠛⠛⠷⠶⠶⠶⠤⠤⢤⣤⣤⣤⣤⣤⣤⣤⡤⠤⠴⠶⠶⠶⠶⠿⠟⡛⢛⠉⠉⢀⡀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    ⠀""", flush=True)
    print("""                                                                                  """, flush=True)
    print("**************************************************************************************", flush=True)
```

**Python:**

```python
def print_python():
    print("******************************************", flush=True)
    print("""                                      """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣤⣴⣶⣶⣶⣶⣶⣦⣄⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢀⣾⠟⠛⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢸⣿⣄⣀⣼⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⢀⣀⣀⣀⡀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠈⠉⠉⠉⠉⠉⠉⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣦⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⣠⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠀⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢰⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠿⠿⠿⠿⠿⠿⠿⠿⠋⠀⣼⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠉⢀⣠⣤⣤⣤⣤⣤⣤⣤⣴⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⢸⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠘⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡇⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⠋⠁⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠈⠛⠻⠿⠿⠇⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⠿⠿⣿⡇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣧⣀⣀⣿⠇⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""    ⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠘⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠋⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀    """, flush=True)
    print("""                                      """, flush=True)
    print("******************************************", flush=True)
```

**Galão da massa:**

```python
def print_galo():
    print("**************************************", flush=True)
    print(""" ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠛⠛⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿ """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⡿⠿⠋⣀⠴⠦⣀⠙⠿⢿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⡏⠉⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⠉⢁⣠⠖⠋⠄⠄⠄⠄⠙⠲⣄⡈⠉⠛⠛⠛⠛⠛⠉⢹ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⠇⢸⠉⠉⠉⠉⣉⣀⠄⠄⠄⠄⠄⣀⠄⠄⠄⠄⢀⣀⠄⠉⣉⠉⠉⠉⡇⢸ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⡄⢸⠄⠄⢠⣾⠉⠉⠁⠄⠄⠄⣰⡏⣆⠄⠄⠄⢸⡟⣇⣸⣿⠄⠄⠄⡇⢸ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⡇⢸⠄⠄⠄⠛⠤⠖⠂⠄⠄⠠⠟⠛⠻⠆⠄⠄⠸⠇⠻⠟⠿⠄⠄⠄⡇⢸ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⣧⠈⡶⠶⠶⠶⢶⡶⠶⠶⠶⣶⠶⠶⠶⠶⣶⠶⠶⠶⢶⡶⠶⠶⠶⢶⠄⣼ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⣿⡄⣇⠄⠄⠄⢸⡇⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⢸⡇⠄⠄⠄⣸⢠⣿ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⣿⣿⠘⡆⠄⠄⢸⡇⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⢸⡇⠄⠄⢰⠃⣿⣿ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⣿⣿⣆⠙⣆⠄⢸⡇⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⢸⡇⠄⣰⠋⣰⣿⣿ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⣿⣿⣿⣦⠘⢦⢸⡇⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⢸⡇⡴⠃⣴⣿⣿⣿ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣀⢾⡇⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⢸⡷⣀⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿ """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣄⠙⢆⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⠄⠄⣿⠄⠄⡰⠋⣠⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣄⠙⣄⣿⠄⠄⠄⠄⣿⣠⠋⣠⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿ """, flush=True)
    print(""" ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣌⠙⠢⣄⣠⠔⠋⣡⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿ """, flush=True) 
    print(""" ⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣷⣦⣌⣡⣴⣾⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿⣿ """, flush=True)
    print("**************************************", flush=True)
```

**PUC Minas (width 75):**

```python
def print_pucminas75():
    print("*********************************************************************", flush=True)
    print("""                                                                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                -:                               """, flush=True)      
    print("""                               --=-                              """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                ::                               """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                ::                               """, flush=True)      
    print("""                               :--.                              """, flush=True)      
    print("""                              -    :                             """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             :      :                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                            ::-:-::-.:                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                           .:-:----:=:                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                   .       :::::::.: .::                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                  - =     ::.::::.: : ::     . :                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                   - -    -.-.:=.::::::-    .  .                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                  - - -   - .:. . :: --:.  :  .:                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                 -   = :  .. :- :    .:-: - ..  .                """, flush=True)      
    print("""                -     - : .      .      :- .    = :              """, flush=True)      
    print("""               :   : - - .::::--::-:::::- : :  .   -             """, flush=True)      
    print("""              =   . - . : ..  -   :.   - -  -..-                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""               -   : -   :  . - :. :  - -   :  -   .             """, flush=True)      
    print("""                -..:.-   ... :- -- - : --   --- -.               """, flush=True)      
    print("""                  -   ::-   . = -- :: -  ---   :                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                  -   .      : --- . :     -   :                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                   :  -      :: -.. =      :  -                  """, flush=True)      
    print("""            :..:.   .-:.....................:-    -..-           """, flush=True)      
    print("""            . - -:.   :                         -- .: .          """, flush=True)      
    print("""            .--    =..-                     ..:.  =:.--          """, flush=True)      
    print("""            -: =-   ::=                    . -   ..:-.           """, flush=True)      
    print("""              .. .    =         : :        .     - :.=           """, flush=True)      
    print("""             :-. .    -      : == == .     :     . - :           """, flush=True)      
    print("""             -----    :     :=::= = ==.    :     =---=           """, flush=True)      
    print("""            .:-===    .    =:.= + +.= --   -    .=-=-:           """, flush=True)      
    print("""            ---:-:        :==:-:+ --.===   -     --:--           """, flush=True)      
    print("""             .: :.        -.:+ -= :+.=..-  =     :...            """, flush=True)      
    print("""             .::     ...     ..=- .=-      --     :::            """, flush=True)      
    print("""            -    :  .. .     ..=- .=-      - -   - . .           """, flush=True)      
    print("""           : -  :. .:..:  :  = -= :+.=  -  .-- -- : ..:          """, flush=True)      
    print("""           =    : -  - :  -==--:+ --.===.   .  --:   -           """, flush=True)      
    print("""           = .  =   :  -   +: = + +.= -=     .-  .   -.          """, flush=True)      
    print("""            . -:     : -    :=-:= = ==.   . -      -: -          """, flush=True)      
    print("""           .  :   -.: :-     - == == -    .: -.:   .. -          """, flush=True)      
    print("""           :.    .   - -       :- -.      :-.   - -  - .         """, flush=True)      
    print("""            =   :    -                    --.   -      -         """, flush=True)      
    print("""           :.     ::- - :                - . ::-  -  -           """, flush=True)      
    print("""           .  : .:: .-   :.             -   .: .-- .. -          """, flush=True)      
    print("""             -:-           ::.      .:-           :--:           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""    =**-.  -=   ==   :**-      :.   =   *                        """, flush=True)      
    print("""    **:=*+ +*   ++  *+:.+      +*  :*   +                        """, flush=True)       
    print("""    **  +* +*   ++ =*          **  **: ++  +.**:  .**=   +*+     """, flush=True)       
    print("""    **  ** +*   ++ *+         .**- **= .*. *+ .*:    +* *+ .     """, flush=True)       
    print("""    ****+  +*   ++ *+         -*:*-*=+  *. *=  *= .**** .*+.     """, flush=True)       
    print("""    **     +*   ++ +*         ++ **::*  *. *=  *= *: .*   =*:    """, flush=True)       
    print("""    **     :*+:+*.  **::*:    *- =*  *. *. *=  *= *:.** ...*=    """, flush=True)       
    print("""    +*      .+++     =++-     +.  -  +- +. +-  += .++ +:.++-     """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                                                 """, flush=True)       
    print("*********************************************************************", flush=True)                                                                                                                       
```                                                                           
                                                                        
**PUC Minas (width 100):**                                                                           

```python
def print_pucminas100():
    print("*********************************************************************************************", flush=True)                                               
    print("""                                            ..                                           """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                           --.-=                                         """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                           :-.::                                         """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                            ..                                           """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                            -=                                           """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                           =---.                                         """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                         .-     :                                        """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                        :.       :                                       """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                       : -  : =  .:.                                     """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                      :.. .-...:=:-=                                     """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                      -.-.-..-.-::-.                                     """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                     - -:.:  :. : :=:=                                   """, flush=True)       
    print("""                          .=         -  -: -- := .:  :.        =:                        """, flush=True)       
    print("""                          . :       ..: :: =- :- -: : .       -  .                       """, flush=True)       
    print("""                          :. :.     :-:-:::-:::::::::::      -  =                        """, flush=True)       
    print("""                          -:: .:    = ..: - .  :.  == =     -  --                        """, flush=True)       
    print("""                         =  .:  :   -:- - : - .  :.  ..   .:  -  -                       """, flush=True)       
    print("""                        -    .: .:  .:: . . : -  -.  : . .:  -    -                      """, flush=True)       
    print("""                       . -     -  : :    .   :.         .: .:    .. .                    """, flush=True)       
    print("""                     .:.:       -  -=.................-:. :.      :..:                   """, flush=True)       
    print("""                    ..    == --  =  =    - =   : -    -. -. =- --     -                  """, flush=True)       
    print("""                    -     = - =   =  =   .. . :  :   -  =   + : +     -                  """, flush=True)       
    print("""                     -    .- ..    =  -  .. = =  .  -  -     - .:    =                   """, flush=True)       
    print("""                      -  :. -.-     =  -  . = - .  -  =.    + -. -  -                    """, flush=True)       
    print("""                       :-  - ..    - :. :.. - : . -  = :.    . .: --                     """, flush=True)       
    print("""                         .:    = =:   :  :. - :  =  =    = =     -                       """, flush=True)       
    print("""                         ..    -       .. :.- : =  -       =     -                       """, flush=True)       
    print("""                          .-   :.       .: .= -- .:        -   .:                        """, flush=True)       
    print("""                   ::       - ::........-:-.:--.:--........:= :.      ::                 """, flush=True)       
    print("""                  =   -.     =                              .=      =   :                """, flush=True)       
    print("""                 -  .  ::.     .                                 .:=  .  =               """, flush=True)       
    print("""                 -.:..:   -::::-                           .::::-.  = --.:               """, flush=True)       
    print("""                 -=  -.    ::  =                           .  .-    -=: =-               """, flush=True)       
    print("""                 ..: = =     = +                           : =     - + - :               """, flush=True)       
    print("""                  = --  .      +                           -       : ...=                """, flush=True)       
    print("""                  . -=  -      +          -+=.-=+.         =      .  -- -                """, flush=True)       
    print("""                  :-:.. -      =       .=. ==.-== -=       =      .....-=                """, flush=True)       
    print("""                  -=-:::=      :       :== ==.-= :=+       -      --:::==                """, flush=True)       
    print("""                  =--::==      .     :-  =- =.-+ +=  =     -      ==-::--                """, flush=True)       
    print("""                  ::--==-            +=+.:+ +.--.= :===    :      :===--:                """, flush=True)       
    print("""                  :=-=---           :=+== = =.-.=-.==+=.   :      :-:-==-                """, flush=True)       
    print("""                       .-      ..   -   +:-:-.- + ==   :   -      .:                     """, flush=True)       
    print("""                    ..        :.:        -.-:.- = +        .=        ..                  """, flush=True)       
    print("""                  -.   -     :. :        =.=:.- + -       .. -     -.  .-                """, flush=True)       
    print("""                 - .--: -  --. --       .-.-:.- + +       .-  --  - .--: -               """, flush=True)       
    print("""                ....   - ::  -= =   =  .=:-:-.- + -=  .:  : -:. = ...   - -              """, flush=True)       
    print("""                - +    - -=  .. =   :==== = +.-.-- ====   :  :  =: =    - -              """, flush=True)       
    print("""                : =    =    --  -    === :+ +.-= = :+=-   -  --  . -    = -              """, flush=True)       
    print("""                .. -  :.    :-  -    .: :=: =.-+ ==  :    -  ::.    -  :. -              """, flush=True)       
    print("""                 -  ..        - :      === ==.-=..==-     - =        ..  =               """, flush=True)       
    print("""                 -        =.-: +:       +  ==.-== :=      -=  =.-.       ..              """, flush=True)       
    print("""                - .: ::  -   .. .         -==.-==.        -: -   .  .- .- -              """, flush=True)       
    print("""                - .   .  .    : :.                        :.      : :    ...             """, flush=True)       
    print("""                :.     : -   ..  -                       : : -   .       - .             """, flush=True)       
    print("""                - -   :   = :: +  :                      . -  = -:  =   . .              """, flush=True)       
    print("""                :  =:-  =     -    -                   .:   =     -. =:-. -              """, flush=True)       
    print("""                 :.   .- .-:-:      -:               .-      ::::: ::   .-               """, flush=True)       
    print("""                   :::.               :--.       .--:                :::.                """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                                                                         """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                                                                         """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                                                                         """, flush=True)           
    print("""                                                                                         """, flush=True)           
    print("""       -+*=:    .-.    --     -**+         :.    :.    *                                 """, flush=True)          
    print("""       ***+**+  -*.    *+   :**++**        *+    *=   =*-                                """, flush=True)           
    print("""       **   +*. -*.    *+  .*+.            **   .**                                      """, flush=True)           
    print("""       **   -*: -*.    *+  **:            :**=  ***  -++. .+:+**+    +**+-   +**+-       """, flush=True)            
    print("""       **   **. -*.    *+  *+             =***  ***: .=*. .**:.-*+   :..+*: +*- .        """, flush=True)            
    print("""       ******+  -*.    *+  *+             +*-*.-*-*-  -*. .**   **    .::*= =*+          """, flush=True)            
    print("""       **==-    -*.    *+  **             ** *+** **  -*. .**   **  =*+=+*=  =***.       """, flush=True)            
    print("""       **       -*:    *+  **-           :*- -**- +*  -*. .**   ** .*+   *=    :**       """, flush=True)            
    print("""       **       .**- .**=   **=  -*      -*. .**  =*. -*. .**   ** .*+  =*+  .  +*       """, flush=True)            
    print("""       **        -******    .******.     +*   +-  :*= -*. .**   **  +****** -****=       """, flush=True)            
    print("""                    .          .                                                         """, flush=True)            
    print("""                                                                                         """, flush=True)            
    print("""                                                                                         """, flush=True)
    print("*********************************************************************************************", flush=True)
```

**PUC Minas (width 150):**

```python
def print_pucminas150():
    print("************************************************************************************************************************************************", flush=True)         
    print("""                                                                                                                                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                     ..                                                                     """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                    .-=                                                                     """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                    .:-.                                                                    """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                  -.. ...-                                                                  """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                  ===:-==-                                                                  """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                    .:-                                                                     """, flush=True)
    print("""                                                                    .:-                                                                     """, flush=True)
    print("""                                                                    .-=.                                                                    """, flush=True)
    print("""                                                                   .-..-.                                                                   """, flush=True)
    print("""                                                                  :=::::-:                                                                  """, flush=True)
    print("""                                                                 =:       -                                                                 """, flush=True)
    print("""                                                               :-          :.                                                               """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                              .-            -.                                                              """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                            .:: .  .:  ::  : ::                                                             """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                            =- :=  --. == .=. =.                                                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                           ..:.- -.: -:..:- :..-                                                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                           :..-: -=  ==  =- -= ..                                                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                          .-:--::-:::-=:::--::--- :                                                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                         .+ .-- ::=  -.- ..- ..-.-+                                                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                          --             := - -.-.:..: - - - ..:.=-.            .-:                                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                         -..+            ::.- :.=  --  :.: ..: ..:.:            = :-                                        """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                         -  .-           -.-: .::  --  .:.  ::  ::.-          .-   =                                        """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                         :-   +.         --::::::-:::--::::-:--:::=:.        .-   -.                                        """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                          =-   -.       --  :-:  .--.   .--.  .--. -:       :-   --                                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                         -.:=   =.      =-  : :  ...:   -. =  .--. =:      .-   =.:-                                        """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                        -.  :-   -:     =...: -  -  -   -  -  -  =:::     :-  .=.  :-                                       """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                       =     .+   -:    :..:  :. =  :. ..  .. :  -- -    -:   =     .+                                      """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                      :-      .-.  ::  .:.::   -::  .: ..  .:.:  -= -   -:  .=.      -.                                     """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                       :.       +.  :- .: :.    .    .=:    ..      -  =.  .=       ::                                      """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                   :--:-.        -.  :- -                           : -.  :-        :-:--:                                  """, flush=True)       
    print("""                                  -:  .           =:  .==::::::::::::::::::::::::::::=.  :-              ::                                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                 -:      :-:  --:  -:  .=.......=..=....--.::.......-.  --  :--  --:      :-                                """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                -.       - :-=  +   --   =      =. -.   =  -.      =   -:   - .+=. +       .:                               """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                .-       .- :. -.    :-  .-.    -: .:  .-  =     .-   -:    :- ...-.      .-.                               """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                 .+       -:  =:      :=   =    :-  =  :.  =    .=   =.      ::  -:       =                                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                  .-     -: .. -.      :-   -.  .-  =  -.  =   :-   -.      :- .. :-    .=.                                 """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                    +   +. .-= ::      .==   -. .-  -: =   =  :-   ==       -..==. .-   -                                   """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                     -.-  :-  --      .- .-.  -:.-  :: =   = ::  .- .-.      -:  -: .-:=                                    """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                      :  -:      :=- :-    =   :=-  :-.=   =-:  .=    -: =+:      -:  .                                     """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                        -:       - .-:      -.  :-  :-.=   =:  .-      --. =       -:                                       """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                        -:       -           -.  :- :- =  =.  :-           +       ::                                       """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                         -:      ::           -:  :-=. =.-.  :-           -.      :-                                        """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                          :-     -.            -:  .+  -=.  -:            :=     =:                                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                               ..          :-   =:.............=--..:-.-...--=.............:-   -.         ...                              """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             .=::-=-         - -=--------------------------------------------=.=.        -=-::=                             """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             -     .-:       .-.+                                           : -        :-.     =                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                            =.       --.        =.                                          :        .--        -                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                            +  :-=  -:.:-:      -.                                         .:      :-:.-: .+=.  -                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                           .=::- - ::    :=-::::=:                                         :-:::::=.    -  +.=:.-                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                            =-:. -::-     .-.   ::                                         :.   .-.     - := :-:-                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                            =.-:  .:-:      :-  .-                                         -. .=:      ::-:  -: -                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                            .- :.:-: -        -::-                                         -::-        = :=.:: =.                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             -. +::  :.         :-                                         =:         -.  - - :.                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             .- =.+   =          -                :-== .=-:.               =          -   - - -                             """, flush=True)      
    print("""                              + :-+   +          -               .==== .====               +          -   -:: -                             """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             .=:.::   +          -           .--  ==== .==+. .=:           +          -   ::.-=                             """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             .=::-=-===          -          :===- .+== .==- .====          =          -=--=-::=                             """, flush=True)     
    print("""                             ::=-::-:-=:         -           :==+. === .==. ===-          .-         ---:-:-===                             """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             -:---:--==-         :        :-  .=== :== .== .==:  .-       .-         ==+-=-:=:-:                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             :=---:-:=::         :       .==+: .==..== .=- ==- .=+=-      ::         --=-:-:=:-=                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             -+:+---:=:.         :       -====: :+- == .+:.+= .=====.     ::         .-=-:---=:+                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             -=-=:+:=-=          :.     .+====+: == -= .+ :=. ======-     -.          -=---+:+:=                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                              .-=--.=-+          :.     ==-:-=== :+.-= .+ -= .===::-+     -           -+-:.+--..                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                      =          -:     -     ==..=::= .= == -=:    .:    --          :.                                    """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                 .              =::            =: =:.= .= =- +:           -.-              .                                """, flush=True)      
    print("""                              :-=-==:          -..-            -- =:.= .- =:.=.           - :-         .:=--=-.                             """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             -.     .-.      .=.  -            :- =:.= .- =:.=.           -  .-       :-.     :=                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                            =.  .::.  =.  .::-   :=            =: =:.= .- =- +.           =:  .=::   .-  .::.   -                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                           -. .-...:-  -  =.:-  =.+     .     :+..=::= .= =- ==      :    -.-  =:.- .=  -:...-. ::                          """, flush=True)      
    print("""                           - .=     :: :..-  :--. +     =-...-== :+.:= .+ -= :==:...=.    : :-=.  - -. ::     -  +                          """, flush=True)      
    print("""                          .: -       - .-:-   ::  =     :+=====: =+ -= .+ -=. =======     :  :.   -.-  +      :. -.                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                          .: -       -  =-   .::  =.     =====- .+- == .+..+= .=====:    .:  ::.   -=  +      .: :.                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                           : ::      -     .-::   -.     :==+-  ==..== .=- ==: .====     .:   ::-      =      :. -.                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                           -  =.    =.     :=:.   :.      -=.  -== .== .== :==.  -=.     :.   .:=.     .-    .-  +                          """, flush=True)      
    print("""                           :.  :=---.        .:-  ::         .===: -== .==. ===:         :. .=:.        .----:  ::                          """, flush=True)      
    print("""                            +.                 .= .:        :+===  +== .==: :+===        -. -                   -                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                           :-            -::--  .- -         :==  -=== .===  :+-.        -.=. .-::--            -.                          """, flush=True)      
    print("""                           -   -==:     +.   .=  - -             .==== .====  .          =:-  -    .-     -==-.  +                          """, flush=True)      
    print("""                          =. :-.  .-   :.     .- :.-             .-=+= .++=:             +-. -.     ::  .-.  .-. .-                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                          +  -     .+  -       - .:-                 .                   =-  +      .=  -      +  -                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                         .= .:      =. -       - .::.                                   ::-  =      .-  -      -. -                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                         .= .:      =. ::     -: : .=                                   - :: .:     -   :      -. -                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                          +  -     .=   :-. .-:  -  :-                                 -.  =  :-. .-:   -      +  -                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                          -. :-    -  .   -=-   =.   ::                               -:   .:   -=-   . .=    -  .:                         """, flush=True)      
    print("""                          -  .::::. .--.     .-.     :-                            .-:     :-.     .--  .::::. .=                           """, flush=True)     
    print("""                           .=.      .=  ==:.:==         =:                         -=         =-:.:=-  +.       =                           """, flush=True)      
    print("""                             :-:.::-:     ...            .--:.                 .:-:.            ...     :-:..:-:                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                               .::.                         :=+-:...........:-+-.                         .::.                              """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                .:::::::::::.                                                               """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                                                                                            """, flush=True)      
    print("""                                                                                                                                            """, flush=True)

    print("""                                                                                                                                            """, flush=True)

    print("""            -**+=++***+.  :**-      =**-    -+**+===+*.           :**:     -*+.    :**-                                                     """, flush=True)

    print("""            -**:    :**=  :**-      =**-   +**-                   +**+.   -***-   ::::.   ::. :---.      .----:.      .----.                """, flush=True)

    print("""            -**:          :**-      =**-  -**=                  :**- .**+**  +*+   .**-   =**     =**   +*+-. .***.    :=***-               """, flush=True)      
    print("""            -**:          .**=      ***:   ***:                 -**:  +***-  =*+.  .**-   =**     =**  :**-    ***.      .***               """, flush=True)

    print("""                                                                                                                                            """, flush=True)
    print("************************************************************************************************************************************************", flush=True)
```
